[30;1m273 | [0m[35mclass ControlTerm(AbstractTerm[_VF, _Control]):[0m
[30;1m274 | [0m[35m    r"""A term representing the general case of $f(t, y(t), args) \mathrm{d}x(t)$, in[0m

[30;1m13 | [0m[35mclass Event(eqx.Module):[0m
[30;1m14 | [0m[35m    """Can be used to terminate the solve early if a condition, or one of multiple[0m
[30;1m15 | [0m[35m    conditions, is triggered. It allows for both boolean and continuous condition[0m
